lɛ ha --entry is a sub-entry and also a separate entry. lɛ ha subentry has additional unmarked sub-entries
    Compound: lɛ ɔmɛ ‘abort a pregnancy’; lɛ ɔnɔ ‘answer’. lɛ mʋ ɔnɔ answer him. Compund: lɛ ɔwan ‘make public’. lɛ kɔ get into debt. Read: Stewart List:3207

\v 42MRK:15:40:04NKO: Atsɩ akʋ ɛ́ bʋlɩɩ́ ɩfʋ́ntɔ́ bʋdɛkɩ́ɩ sɩsɩ́.
Is this sɩsɩ́ (LH) the same as sɩsɩ (LL) in the dictionary?
e.g. Bapʋ nkla sɩsɩ mɩ ánɩ́ mba.
If they are the same:
	Which one is correct?
	What other verbs besides kɩ  & pʋ can take sɩsɩ ?
If they are different
	Which other verbs besides kɩ can take sɩsɩ́ ?

Q: Nfɩ brɛʋʋ! A: Anɩmɛdɛ tsitsa! Q: Things are gentle here (We are fine. Implies: How are you?) A: We don't have any bad news
Q: Ɩnʋ da? A: Tsitsa kʋkʋ ma nʋ. Q: How are things there? A: There is no bad news.

brɛʋʋ needs entry
1) softly / gently
Nfɩ brɛʋʋ! Literally: Things are gentle here. Implied question: Why have you come?

\v 59HEB:01:06:04NKO: Ɩ́nɩ ɔma asa Bulu ɔbɔ́wa mʋ Bitɩ́ ámʋ . . .
\v 59HEB:01:06:05NKN: Ɩnɩ ɔma asa Bulu ɔbɔ́wa mʋ Bitɩ amʋ . . .
In our dictionary and in Deuteronomy & Psalms we have bitɩ spelled bite which is correct?
This is correct for firstborn.
Bite refers to a lady. That is why she is called obitebi. So we have to put both in the dictionary.
That of a male is yasʋ, that is why he is also called ɔyasubi.

oloku not in dictionary also at I Cor 10:3

In the dictionary, we have 4 different meaning for kɛn:
kɛn1   [kɛ̃́(H)] ADJ. the same as. Category: identity TN I.C.1.b. Variant: gyein ‘South’. Amʋ́ kɛn dɛpʋ mlɩ ya asʋn ogyikpa nɩ. These are the same ones who are taking you to court. [Tape:3-1-469] Mɩ atadɩɛ amʋ kɛn nɩ. This is the same shirt that I wore. Mɩ atadɩɛ amʋ kɛn mʋ ɛ ɔlɔwa nɩ. My shirt is the same as the one he is wearing. [Tape:3-1-472] Mʋ kɛn lɛba nfɩ igye nɩ. He is the same one who came yesterday. [Tape:3-1-475] Omefi mʋ́ asɩ wanklaan, alɩ kɛn ɔbʋ mʋ́sʋ nɩ. He didn't start well so he is continuing in the same way.
kɛn2   [kɛ̃́(H)] ADV. indeed; for sure. Category: communication TN II.B.2. Ɩlehian ánɩ́ abówun Igna kɛn. Without a doubt, it is necessary we see Igna. [Tape:3-1-478] Ndɛ mʋ́ ɔkpa kɩ ánɩ́ bɛ́ba kɛn. By all means, I am expecting it. I am certain it will happen. [Tape:3-1-479]
kɛn3   [kɛ̃ʔ(L)] v. to grunt. Category: Uncategorized TN ZZ.
kɛn4   [kɛ̃ʔ(L)] v. to become larger. Category: logic TN I.C.5.

Is kɛɩn in:

\v 59HEB:11:12:05NKN: Ɩnɩ sʋ ɔmá kɛɩn ánɩ́ ...

\v 94XXA:00:0055:04NKO:\p \k Esau\k* \tl Esau\tl* Abraham mʋ bi Isak lɔ́kwɩɩ́ atabí ayin anyɔ. Bɛtɩ amʋ́ Esau mʋa Yakob. Esau gyí ɔhandɛ, támɛ ɛkɛ ɔkʋá akʋ́n lɛkɩtá mʋ a, ɔlɛfɛ mʋ ɩkwɩ́ɩ-dɛhɛn há mʋ gyama Yakob. Olotsulá ánɩ́ Yakob otsúu mʋ handɛ oyúla, ɔha mʋ mpʋ-wʋ́dɩ́ ogyi. Yakob abí-aná Bulu lɔ́pʋbwɛ́ mʋ ahá, megyí Esau klɛ́. Yɛkɩ \w Abraham\w*. (Rom. 9:10-13; Heb. 11:20; 12:16-17).

\v 94XXA:00:0087:04NKO:\p \k Ɩwɩtɩ́ɩn\k* \tl Purity\tl* Yudafɔ amándɩ́ɛ́ ɔnɔ́ á, fɔpʋ́ ɩbɩ da fúli pʋ́ atogyihɛ ɩkʋ aná, ntɛ́ɛ ɩlɔ pɛpɛ ɔlɔpʋ́ á, ifin lada fʋ Mose mbla ámʋ ɔkpasʋ. Alɩ kɛ́n igyi nɩ́ ɔtsɩ ɔkwɩ́ɩ́, ntɛ́ɛ ɔdálɩ omuá mʋ ɩwɩ mɛtɩn amándɩ́ɛ́ ámʋ ɔnɔ́ nɩ́. Ɔhá ánɩ́ mʋ ɩwɩ lɛ́tɩn gyí ɔha anɩ́ mbusuo kʋkʋ má mʋ ɩwɩ. Mʋbʋ́ʋ ɔkpa bwɛ́ osum agyʋ́má ɔtswɛ́kpa ɩnʋ. Támɛ Bulu Ntam Pɔpwɛ amʋ ɔkpasʋ á, alɩ amándɩ́ɛ́ ánfɩ mɛklɩ́ ɔtsɩá alakwɩ́ɩ́ ntɛ́ɛ aladálɩ omuá. (2 Ko. 6:6; Efe. 5:3).
\v 94XXA:00:0087:05NKN:\p \k Ɩwɩtɩn\k* \tl Purity\tl* Yudafɔ amandɩɛ ɔnɔ a, fɔpʋ ɩbɩ da fuli pʋ́ atogyihɛ ɩkʋ aná, ntɛ ɩlɔ pɛpɛ ɔlɔpʋ a, ifin lada fʋ Mose mbla amʋ ɔkpasʋ. Alɩ kɛn igyi nɩ ɔtsɩ ɔkwɩɩ, ntɛ ɔdalɩ omua mʋ ɩwɩ mɛtɩn amandɩɛ amʋ ɔnɔ nɩ. Ɔha ánɩ́ mʋ ɩwɩ lɛtɩn gyi ɔha anɩ́ mbusuo kʋkʋ má mʋ ɩwɩ. Mʋbʋ ɔkpa bwɛ osum agyʋma ɔtswɛkpa ɩnʋ. Tamɛ Bulu Ntam Pɔpwɛ amʋ ɔkpasʋ a, alɩ amandɩɛ anfɩ mɛklɩ ɔtsɩá alakwɩɩ ntɛ aladalɩ omua. (2 Ko. 6:6; Efe. 5:3).
